Users log sets, see progress, and get guided to their next session automatically.\n    17→\n    18→**Coach-optional model:** Users with `coach_id IS NULL` get zero coach UI.     → /login         Public\n    49→  (auth)/signup         → /signup        Public\n    50→  auth/callback         → OAuth callback  Public\n    51→  (app)/dashboard       → /dashboard `supabase/migrations/001_initial_schema.sql`. Key tables:\n    66→- `profiles` — extends auth.users, has `role`, `gender`, `coach_id`, `template_tier`\n    67→- `session_logs` — one per user per session, tracks effort/soreness\n    68→- `set_logs` — one per set logged\n    69→- `coach_form_assessments` — **NEVER exposed to user role** — internal coach tool\n    70→- `coach_notes` — banner + history system\n    71→- `template_exercises` — weight defaults for all 6 tier/gender combos\n    72→\n    73→### RBAC\n    74→- **admin** — full access, creates users/coaches, edits program templates\n    75→- **coach** — sees own clients, sends notes, marks form assessments\n    76→- **user** — sees own data only, never sees form scores (only \"Solid Form ✅\" on locked_in)\n    77→\n    78→---\n    79→\n    80→## Design tokens (globals.css)\n    81→\n    82→```\n    83→bg-base:       #EDE4D3   page background (warm parchment)\n    84→bg-surface:    #E5DAC8   sidebar, sticky headers\n    85→bg-elevated:   #E8DECE   cards, panels\n    86→bg-hover:      #DDD2BF   hover states\n    87→\n    88→border-subtle: #C8B99D\n    89→border-strong: #B5A68C\n    90→\n    91→content-primary:   #2C1A10   (deep brown)\n    92→content-secondary: #6B5A48   (warm brown)\n    93→content-muted:     #988A78   (soft brown)\n    94→\n    95→brand:       #1C3A2A   (forest green — accent only)\n    96→accent:      #C84B1A   (burnt orange — CTAs, highlights)\n    97→accent-dim:  #8C3410\n    98→button-text: #FEFCF8   (warm white — on accent buttons)\n    99→\n   100→success:     #2D7A3A\n   101→warning:     #C08030\n   102→error:       #B83020\n   103→```\n   104→\n   105→App name rendering (must match everywhere):\n   106→```tsx\n   107→<span style={{ color: \"#1C3A2A\" }}>Build</span>\n   108→<span style={{ color: \"#C84B1A\", fontWeight: 700 }}>Base</span>\n   109→```\n   110→\n   111→---\n   112→\n   113→## Key UX rules (non-negotiable)\n   114→\n   115→1. **Form scores NEVER shown to users** — `coach_form_assessments` is coach-only. User sees only \"Solid Form ✅\" badge when `status === 'locked_in'`. Use `getFormBadge()` from `lib/utils.ts`.\n   116→2. **Session tracker pagination** — 3 sessions per page (`SESSIONS_PER_PAGE`), next incomplete auto-opens, completed auto-collapse.\n   117→3. **Soreness prompt** — fires when `hoursSince(lastCompletedAt) > SORENESS_PROMPT_GAP_HOURS (12h)` and `soreness_prompted` is false. Sets `soreness_prompted = true` on dismiss.\n   118→4. **Effort prompt** — after last set of a session. Scale: 1(🔴 Easy)→5(💪 Maxed). Auto-dismisses after 4s.\n   119→5. **Coach notes banner** — shown on dashboard until user hits X (`dismissed_at` is set). Full history at `/coach-notes`.\n   120→6. **Optimistic updates** — set_logs update immediately, sync in background.\n   121→\n   122→---\n   123→\n   124→## Conventions\n   125→\n   126→### Branch naming\n   127→```\n   128→feat/batch-{n}-{short-description}   roadmap batch work\n   129→fix/{short-description}              bug fixes\n   130→chore/{short-description}            deps, config, CI\n   131→```\n   132→\n   133→### Commit format\n   134→```\n   135→type: short description (imperative, lowercase)\n   136→\n   137→Co-Authored-By: Claude Sonnet 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>\n   138→```\n   139→Types: `feat`, `fix`, `chore`, `test`, `docs`\n   140→\n   141→### PR process\n   142→1. Branch off `main`\n   143→2. `pnpm tsc --noEmit` must be clean\n   144→3. `pnpm test` must pass\n   145→4. Update `lib/roadmap-data.ts` with PR number and status\n   146→5. PR targets `main`\n   147→\n   148→---\n   149→\n   150→## Testing\n   151→\n   152→```bash\n   153→pnpm test           # vitest run\n   154→pnpm test:watch     # watch mode\n   155→pnpm test:coverage  # coverage report\n   156→pnpm tsc --noEmit   # type-check only\n   157→```\n   158→\n   159→Tests live in `tests/`. Coverage configured for `lib/**/*.ts`.\n   160→Each roadmap item must have tests before its PR is merged.\n   161→\n   162→---\n   163→\n   164→## Environment variables\n   165→\n   166→| Var | Where | Purpose |\n   167→|-----|-------|---------|\n   168→| `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL` | Vercel + local | Supabase project URL |\n   169→| `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` | Vercel + local | Supabase public anon key |\n   170→| `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` | Vercel (server only) | Bypasses RLS — admin ops only |\n   171→| `ROADMAP_PIN` | Vercel | PIN for /monitor/roadmap |\n   172→| `GITHUB_TOKEN` | Vercel (server only) | PAT (repo + workflow) for kickoff API |\n   173→| `NEXT_PUBLIC_GITHUB_REPO` | Vercel | `omerskywalker/BuildBase` |\n   174→| `NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL` | Vercel | `https://buildbase.io` |\n   175→| `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` | GitHub Actions secrets | Claude Code in CI workflows |\n   176→\n   177→---\n   178→\n   179→## Updating the roadmap monitor\n   180→\n   181→When a PR for a roadmap item is opened:\n   182→1. The product is pre-scaffold but not yet feature-complete — agents are building it batch by batch via the `/monitor/roadmap` kickoff system.\n    17→\n    18→## Data Flow\n    19→\n    20→```\n    21→Browser ──► proxy.ts (auth guard + PIN gate + Supabase session refresh)\n    22→         ──► App Router server components (lib/supabase/server.ts)\n    23→         ──► Supabase PostgreSQL (RLS enforced)\n    24→\n    25→Monitor ──► /monitor/roadmap (server component, reads GitHub PR status + Upstash KV)\n    26→         ──► KickoffButton → POST /api/monitor/kickoff\n    27→         ──► GitHub workflow_dispatch → claude-feature.yml\n    28→         ──► Claude Code agent (reads GitHub Issue for spec, writes code, commits, pushes)\n    29→         ──► PR marked ready → human reviews + merges\n    30→```\n    31→\n    32→## Tech Stack\n    33→\n    34→| Layer | Technology |\n    35→|---|---|\n    36→| Framework | Next.js 16.2.2 — App Router, `proxy.ts` (not `middleware.ts`) |\n    37→| UI | React 19, Tailwind v4 (CSS-first), shadcn/ui v4 (base-nova style) |\n    38→| Auth + DB | Supabase (PostgreSQL + RLS + SSR auth via `@supabase/ssr`) |\n    39→| KV store | Upstash Redis (`@upstash/redis`) — roadmap status overrides only |\n    40→| Charts | Recharts |\n    41→| Animation | Framer Motion |\n    42→| DnD | dnd-kit (Batch 7) |\n    43→| Toast | Sonner |\n    44→| Server state | TanStack React Query |\n    45→| Client state | Zustand |\n    46→| Tests | Vitest + jsdom |\n    47→| CI | GitHub Actions — `claude-feature.yml` (agent) + `ci.yml` (lint/test) |\n    48→| Hosting | Vercel (auto-deploy `main`; preview on all branches) |\n    49→| Package mgr | pnpm 9 |\n    50→\n    51→## Key Files\n    52→\n    53→| File | Purpose |\n    54→|---|---|\n    55→| `proxy.ts` | Auth guard + monitor PIN gate + Supabase session refresh. Next.js 16 — not middleware.ts |\n    56→| `lib/types.ts` | All shared TypeScript interfaces — Profile, SessionLog, SetLog, CoachNote, etc. |\n    57→| `lib/roadmap-data.ts` | Roadmap item definitions. `status`, `pr`, `issue` updated as work progresses |\n    58→| `lib/storage.ts` | Upstash Redis KV — `getRoadmapOverrides()` / `setRoadmapOverride()`. Key: `bb:roadmap-overrides` |\n    59→| `lib/github-api.ts` | GitHub REST helpers: `ensureBranchReady`, `createDraftPr`, `createIssue`, `getMainSha` |\n    60→| `lib/supabase/server.ts` | Server  → /reset-password  Public\n    78→  auth/callback           → OAuth callback   Public\n    79→  (app)/dashboard         → /dashboard       Protected: all roles\n    80→  (app)/sessions          →       → PIN gate         Public\n    89→  monitor/roadmap         → Dev monitor      PIN-gated\n    90→```\n    91→\n    92→## Database Schema (key tables)\n    93→\n    94→| Table | Purpose |\n    95→|---|---|\n    96→| `profiles` | Extends auth.users — `role`, `gender`, `coach_id`, `template_tier`, `onboarding_done` |\n    97→| `programs` / `phases` | Program definitions — 3 phases, 12 weeks |\n    98→| `workout_templates` | Per-week session templates (36 per program) |\n    99→| `template_exercises` | Exercises with 6 weight defaults (3 tiers × 2 genders) |\n   100→| `user_enrollments` | Links user to program + tracks current week/session |\n   101→| `session_logs` | One per user per session — effort, soreness, completion |\n   102→| `set_logs` | One per set logged — weight_used, `personal_records` | Auto-detected PRs per exercise |\n   106→| `milestones` | Achievement tracking |\n   107→\n   108→## KV Store\n   109→\n   110→| Key | Type | Purpose |\n   111→|---|---|---|\n   112→| `bb:roadmap-overrides` | `Record<string, RoadmapOverride>` | Runtime status/pr/issue overrides for roadmap monitor items. Bypasses static `roadmap-data.ts` so clicking \"Start\" immediately shows in-progress without redeploy |\n   113→\n   114→`RoadmapOverride = { status: \"in-progress\" \\| \"done\" \\| \"paused\", pr?: number, issue?: number, startedAt?: string }`\n   115→\n   116→Requires env vars: `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL` + `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN` (Vercel env).\n   117→Degrades gracefully to static data when not configured.\n   118→\n   119→## Environment Variables\n   120→\n   121→| Variable | Where set | Purpose |\n   122→|---|---|---|\n   123→| `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL` | Vercel + local | Supabase {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_011fcAWBrXnKLgNu3U64UAq7","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→---\n     2→type: gotchas\n     3→tags: [gotchas, lessons-learned, buildbase]\n     4→last-updated: 2026-04-16\n     5→---\n     6→\n     7→# Gotchas — BuildBase\n     8→\n     9→> Read this before starting any task. Each entry is a real thing that burned us.\n    10→> Add new entries at the top with the date.\n    11→\n    12→---\n    13→\n    14→## 2026-04-24 — Test files with JSX must use .tsx extension\n    15→\n    16→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with dozens of `'>' expected`, `',' expected`, and `Expression expected` errors in test files.\n    17→\n    18→**Cause:** TypeScript cannot parse JSX syntax (`<Component />`) in `.ts` files. The file must have a `.tsx` extension for JSX to be valid. This has burned us on items 3-2 and 3-3 — both times the agent wrote React component render tests in a `.ts` file.\n    19→\n    20→**Rule for test files:**\n    21→- If a test **imports and renders React components** (uses `render()`, JSX, `screen.*`) → name it `*.test.tsx`\n    22→- If a test **only tests pure functions, data transforms, and logic** (no JSX) → name it `*.test.ts`\n    23→\n    24→Most BuildBase tests should be `.test.ts` because coverage targets `lib/**/*.ts` (pure logic). Prefer testing the logic the component uses, not rendering the component itself. Only write `.tsx` tests when you specifically need to test interactive UI behavior.\n    25→\n    26→---\n    27→\n    28→## 2026-04-16 — TypeScript strict mode: never initialize array/object state with null\n    29→\n    30→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with `Type 'null' is not assignable to type 'OptimisticSet'` (or similar). Commit step is blocked, PR ends up with 0 files changed.\n    31→\n    32→**Cause:** `strictNullChecks` is on. `useState<T>(null)` is only valid if the type is `T | null`. Initializing array state with `null` instead of `[]` causes a hard TS error.\n    33→\n    34→**Fix:**\n    35→```ts\n    36→// WRONG — TS2322 in strict mode\n    37→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>(null)\n    38→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog>(null)\n    39→\n    40→// CORRECT\n    41→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>([])\n    42→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog | null>(null)\n    43→```\n    44→When null IS a valid value, add `| null` to the type. When it's an empty collection, start with `[]`.\n    45→\n    46→---\n    47→\n    48→## 2026-04-16 — claude-code-action@beta requires `mode: agent` + `direct_prompt`\n    49→\n    50→**Symptom:** Workflow run fails immediately with:\n    51→`Error: Prepare step failed with error: Tag mode cannot handle workflow_dispatch events. Use 'agent' mode for automation events.`\n    52→\n    53→**Cause:** `claude-code-action@beta` changed its API. The old input `prompt:` is no longer valid — it must be `direct_prompt:`. And `workflow_dispatch` events require `mode: agent` to be set explicitly (default mode is \"tag\" which only works on PR/issue events).\n    54→\n    55→**Fix:**\n    56→```yaml\n    57→- uses: anthropics/claude-code-action@beta\n    58→  with:\n    59→    anthropic_api_key: ${{ secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY }}\n    60→    mode: agent          # ← required for workflow_dispatch\n    61→    direct_prompt: |     # ← not \"prompt:\"\n    62→      ...\n    63→```\n    64→\n    65→---\n    66→\n    67→## 2026-04-16 — ANTHROPIC_API_KEY must be in GitHub Actions secrets (not just Vercel)\n    68→\n    69→**Symptom:** After fixing the mode error, workflow fails with:\n    70→`Error: Environment variable validation failed: Either ANTHROPIC_API_KEY or CLAUDE_CODE_OAUTH_TOKEN is required when using direct Anthropic API.`\n    71→\n    72→**Cause:** `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is set as a Vercel env var (for any future server-side AI use) but GitHub Actions has its own separate secrets store. The workflow's `secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` looks in the repo's Actions secrets, not Vercel.\n    73→\n    74→**Fix:** Go to GitHub → repo → Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions → New repository secret → `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`.\n    75→\n    76→---\n    77→\n    78→## 2026-04-16 — GitHub workflow file: merge conflicts silently drop critical lines\n    79→\n    80→**Symptom:** PR was merged, but `mode: agent` and `direct_prompt:` still weren't on main. The old `prompt:` key survived.\n    81→\n    82→**Cause:** When multiple PRs touched `.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml`, the merge conflict was resolved back to the old version. GitHub's merge commit silently kept the old field names.\n    83→\n    84→**Fix:** After any PR touching `claude-feature.yml`, always verify with `git show origin/main:.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml | grep -E \"mode:|direct_prompt:|prompt:\"` before triggering a kickoff.\n    85→\n    86→---\n    87→\n    88→## 2026-04-16 — Issue numbers must be stamped in roadmap-data.ts before kickoff\n    89→\n    90→**Symptom:** Clicking \"Start\" creates a new duplicate GitHub Issue every time, even when the issue already exists.\n    91→\n    92→**Cause:** `createIssue()` is guarded by `item.issue ?? existing?.issue ?? null`. If `item.issue` is `undefined` in `roadmap-data.ts` AND Upstash Redis is not configured (so `existing` is always `{}`), the guard fails and a new issue is created unconditionally on every click.\n    93→\n    94→**Fix:** All issue numbers are now stamped in `lib/roadmap-data.ts` (items 1-1 through 7-3 → GitHub issues #17–40). Never remove these numbers. Duplicate issues #42–44, #47 were closed.\n    95→\n    96→---\n    97→\n    98→## 2026-04-16 — Workflow commit step silently succeeds with 0 changes\n    99→\n   100→**Symptom:** PR is marked \"ready for review\" but has 0 file changes — only the empty init commit.\n   101→\n   102→**Cause:** The commit step had `|| echo \"Nothing to commit\"` which swallowed the git failure. Then `git push` pushed the empty branch and `gh pr ready` marked it done. The Claude Code agent may have written nothing (model/auth issue) but the workflow appeared to succeed.\n   103→\n   104→**Fix:** Added a \"Verify changes exist\" step before commit:\n   105→```bash\n   106→git add -A\n   107→if git diff --cached --quiet; then\n   108→  echo \"::error::Claude Code produced no file changes.\"\n   109→  exit 1\n   110→fi\n   111→```\n   112→\n   113→---\n   114→\n   115→## 2026-04-15 — GitHub fine-grained PAT needs 4 specific permissions\n   116→\n   117→**Symptom:** `/api/monitor/kickoff` returns `{ \"error\": \"Failed to prepare branch — check GITHUB_TOKEN permissions\" }`.\n   118→\n   119→**Cause:** The fine-grained PAT used as `GITHUB_TOKEN` in Vercel was missing one or more required permissions.\n   120→\n   121→**Required permissions (all must be Read and write):**\n   122→- **Contents** — create branches, create commits via git data API\n   123→- **Pull requests** — create draft PRs\n   124→- **Issues** — create/read GitHub Issues\n   125→- **Actions** — trigger `workflow_dispatch`\n   126→\n   127→---\n   128→\n   129→## 2026-04-15 — Branch must have ≥1 commit ahead of main for PR creation\n   130→\n   131→**Symptom:** `createDraftPr()` returns 422 from GitHub: \"No commits between main and feat/...\".\n   132→\n   133→**Cause:** GitHub requires the head branch to have at least one commit that main doesn't have before a PR can be created. `createBranch()` alone just creates a ref pointing to the same SHA as main — same tree, no diff.\n   134→\n   135→**Fix:** `ensureBranchReady()` in `lib/github-api.ts` calls `createEmptyCommit()` when the branch HEAD SHA equals main's HEAD SHA. This creates a git commit with the same tree but a new hash, satisfying GitHub's requirement.\n   136→\n   137→---\n   138→\n   139→## 2026-04-15 — Upstash Redis env vars required for live in-progress status\n   140→\n   141→**Symptom:** Clicking \"Start\" fires the kickoff API, button shows \"Started → PR\", but the roadmap page never updates to show \"In Progress\" after `router.refresh()`.\n   142→\n   143→**Cause:** `setRoadmapOverride()` in `lib/storage.ts` silently no-ops if `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL` / `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN` are not set. The KV write is skipped, so on the next page render the static `roadmap-data.ts` status (not-started) is still shown.\n   144→\n   145→**Fix:** Set both Upstash env vars in Vercel. The monitor degrades gracefully without them but live status updates don't work.\n   146→\n   147→---\n   148→\n   149→## Next.js 16 — proxy.ts replaces middleware.ts\n   150→\n   151→**Symptom:** Auth guard or session refresh logic silently does nothing.\n   152→\n   153→**Cause:** Next.js 16 renamed `middleware.ts` → `proxy.ts`. The exported function must be named `proxy`, not `middleware`. A `middleware.ts` at the root is silently ignored.\n   154→\n   155→**Fix:**\n   156→```ts\n   157→// CORRECT — proxy.ts\n   158→export async function proxy(request: NextRequest) { ... }\n   159→export const config = { matcher: [...] }; // no `runtime` key — build error\n   160→\n   161→// WRONG — silently no-ops\n   162→export function middleware(request: NextRequest) { ... }\n   163→```\n   164→Note: `runtime` is not allowed in proxy.ts config — it always runs on Node.js.\n   165→\n   166→---\n   167→\n   168→## Next.js 16 — params and cookies/headers are async\n   169→\n   170→**Symptom:** `params.id` is undefined; `cookies()` causes a type error.\n   171→\n   172→**Fix:**\n   173→```ts\n   174→// Pages/layouts\n   175→export default async function Page({ params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }) {\n   176→  const { id } = await params;\n   177→}\n   178→\n   179→// Server components\n   180→const cookieStore = await cookies();\n   181→const headersList = await headers();\n   182→```\n   183→\n   184→---\n   185→\n   186→## Tailwind v4 — no tailwind.config.ts, @theme is CSS-first\n   187→\n   188→**Symptom:** Custom tokens not resolving, or shadcn init breaks fonts.\n   189→\n   190→**Cause:** Tailwind v4 uses CSS-first config. All design tokens live in the `@theme {}` block in `app/globals.css`. Font references inside `@theme` must be literal strings — `var()` references resolve at parse time and can't see Next.js runtime injections.\n   191→\n   192→**Fix:**\n   193→```css\n   194→/* CORRECT */\n   195→--font-sans: \"Inter\", ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif;\n   196→\n   197→/* WRONG — circular */\n   198→--font-sans: var(--font-sans);\n   199→\n   200→/* WRONG — next/font injects this at runtime, @theme can't see it */\n   201→--font-sans: var(--font-inter);\n   202→```\n   203→\n   204→---\n   205→\n   206→## Supabase — getUser() not getSession() in proxy.ts\n   207→\n   208→**Symptom:** Auth seems to work but sessions don't refresh correctly; stale tokens.\n   209→\n   210→**Cause:** `getSession()` reads from the cookie without re-validating against the Supabase auth server. Only `getUser()` re-validates and refreshes the session token.\n   211→\n   212→**Fix:** `proxy.ts` must use `supabase.auth.getUser()`.\n   213→\n   214→---\n   215→\n   216→## Supabase — coach_form_assessments is coach-only, forever\n   217→\n   218→**Symptom:** Form assessment scores visible to users in the UI.\n   219→\n   220→**Cause:** The `coach_form_assessments` table was queried in a user-facing component.\n   221→\n   222→**Fix:** Users NEVER see raw form status. Use `getFormBadge(status)` from `lib/utils.ts`:\n   223→- `locked_in` → `\"Solid Form ✅\"`\n   224→- Everything else → `null`\n   225→RLS on the table also enforces this at the DB level.\n   226→\n   227→---\n   228→\n   229→## Monitor — MONITOR_COOKIE name is the source of truth\n   230→\n   231→The monitor cookie name is `_bb_ok`, defined in `lib/constants.ts` as `MONITOR_COOKIE`. Both `proxy.ts` and `/api/monitor/kickoff/route.ts` parse the raw `Cookie` header for this value. If the name ever changes, update both files.\n   232→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it looks malicious. Does\\n    15→\\n    16→BuildBase is a structured fitness coaching SaaS with RBAC (admin / coach / user). Coaches program 12-week strength plans, track client form, and send notes. Users log sets, view progress, and get automatically guided to their next session. The product is pre-scaffold but not yet feature-complete — agents are building it batch by batch via the `/monitor/roadmap` kickoff system.\\n    17→\\n    18→## Data Flow\\n    19→\\n    20→```\\n    21→Browser ──► proxy.ts (auth guard + PIN gate + Supabase session refresh)\\n    22→         ──► App Router server components (lib/supabase/server.ts)\\n    23→         ──► Supabase PostgreSQL (RLS enforced)\\n    24→\\n    25→Monitor ──► /monitor/roadmap (server component, reads GitHub PR status + Upstash KV)\\n    26→         ──► KickoffButton → POST /api/monitor/kickoff\\n    27→         ──► GitHub workflow_dispatch → claude-feature.yml\\n    28→         ──► Claude Code agent (reads GitHub Issue for spec, writes code, commits, pushes)\\n    29→         ──► PR marked ready → human reviews + merges\\n    30→```\\n    31→\\n    32→## Tech Stack\\n    33→\\n    34→| Layer | Technology |\\n    35→|---|---|\\n    36→| Framework | Next.js 16.2.2 — App Router, `proxy.ts` (not `middleware.ts`) |\\n    37→| UI | React 19, Tailwind v4 (CSS-first), shadcn/ui v4 (base-nova style) |\\n    38→| Auth + DB | Supabase (PostgreSQL + RLS + SSR auth via `@supabase/ssr`) |\\n    39→| KV store | Upstash Redis (`@upstash/redis`) — roadmap status overrides only |\\n    40→| Charts | Recharts |\\n    41→| Animation | Framer Motion |\\n    42→| DnD | dnd-kit (Batch 7) |\\n    43→| Toast | Sonner |\\n    44→| Server state | TanStack React Query |\\n    45→| Client state | Zustand |\\n    46→| Tests | Vitest + jsdom |\\n    47→| CI | GitHub Actions — `claude-feature.yml` (agent) + `ci.yml` (lint/test) |\\n    48→| Hosting | Vercel (auto-deploy `main`; preview on all branches) |\\n    49→| Package mgr | pnpm 9 |\\n    50→\\n    51→## Key Files\\n    52→\\n    53→| File | Purpose |\\n    54→|---|---|\\n    55→| `proxy.ts` | Auth guard + monitor PIN gate + Supabase session refresh. Each entry is a real thing that burned us.\\n    10→> Add new entries at the top with the date.\\n    11→\\n    12→---\\n    13→\\n    14→## 2026-04-24 — Test files with JSX must use .tsx extension\\n    15→\\n    16→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with dozens of `'>' expected`, `',' expected`, and `Expression expected` errors in test files.\\n    17→\\n    18→**Cause:** TypeScript cannot parse JSX syntax (`<Component />`) in `.ts` files. The file must have a `.tsx` extension for JSX to be valid. This has burned us on items 3-2 and 3-3 — both times the agent wrote React component render tests in a `.ts` file.\\n    19→\\n    20→**Rule for test files:**\\n    21→- If a test **imports and renders React components** (uses `render()`, JSX, `screen.*`) → name it `*.test.tsx`\\n    22→- If a test **only tests pure functions, data transforms, and logic** (no JSX) → name it `*.test.ts`\\n    23→\\n    24→Most BuildBase tests should be `.test.ts` because coverage targets `lib/**/*.ts` (pure logic). Prefer testing the logic the component uses, not rendering the component itself. Only write `.tsx` tests when you specifically need to test interactive UI behavior.\\n    25→\\n    26→---\\n    27→\\n    28→## 2026-04-16 — TypeScript strict mode: never initialize array/object state with null\\n    29→\\n    30→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with `Type 'null' is not assignable to type 'OptimisticSet'` (or similar). Commit step is blocked, PR ends up with 0 files changed.\\n    31→\\n    32→**Cause:** `strictNullChecks` is on. `useState<T>(null)` is only valid if the type is `T | null`. Initializing array state with `null` instead of `[]` causes a hard TS error.\\n    33→\\n    34→**Fix:**\\n    35→```ts\\n    36→// WRONG — TS2322 in strict mode\\n    37→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>(null)\\n    38→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog>(null)\\n    39→\\n    40→// CORRECT\\n    41→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>([])\\n    42→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog | null>(null)\\n    43→```\\n    44→When null IS a valid value, add `| null` to the type. When it's an empty collection, start with `[]`.\\n    45→\\n    46→---\\n    47→\\n    48→## 2026-04-16 — claude-code-action@beta requires `mode: agent` + `direct_prompt`\\n    49→\\n    50→**Symptom:** Workflow run fails immediately with:\\n    51→`Error: Prepare step failed with error: Tag mode cannot handle workflow_dispatch events. Use 'agent' mode for automation events.`\\n    52→\\n    53→**Cause:** `claude-code-action@beta` changed its API. The old input `prompt:` is no longer valid — it must be `direct_prompt:`. And `workflow_dispatch` events require `mode: agent` to be set explicitly (default mode is \\\"tag\\\" which only works on PR/issue events).\\n    54→\\n    55→**Fix:**\\n    56→```yaml\\n    57→- uses: anthropics/claude-code-action@beta\\n    58→  with:\\n    59→    anthropic_api_key: ${{ secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY }}\\n    60→    mode: agent          # ← required for workflow_dispatch\\n    61→    direct_prompt: |     # ← not \\\"prompt:\\\"\\n    62→      ...\\n    63→```\\n    64→\\n    65→---\\n    66→\\n    67→## 2026-04-16 — ANTHROPIC_API_KEY must be in GitHub Actions secrets (not just Vercel)\\n    68→\\n    69→**Symptom:** After fixing the mode error, workflow fails with:\\n    70→`Error: Environment variable validation failed: Either ANTHROPIC_API_KEY or CLAUDE_CODE_OAUTH_TOKEN is required when using direct Anthropic API.`\\n    71→\\n    72→**Cause:** `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is set as a Vercel env var (for any future server-side AI use) but GitHub Actions has its own separate secrets store. The workflow's `secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` looks in the repo's Actions secrets, not Vercel.\\n    73→\\n    74→**Fix:** Go to GitHub → repo → Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions → New repository secret → `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`.\\n    75→\\n    76→---\\n    77→\\n    78→## 2026-04-16 — GitHub workflow file: merge conflicts silently drop critical lines\\n    79→\\n    80→**Symptom:** PR was merged, but `mode: agent` and `direct_prompt:` still weren't on main. The old `prompt:` key survived.\\n    81→\\n    82→**Cause:** When multiple PRs touched `.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml`, the merge conflict was resolved back to the old version. GitHub's merge commit silently kept the old field names.\\n    83→\\n    84→**Fix:** After any PR touching `claude-feature.yml`, always verify with `git show origin/main:.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml | grep -E \\\"mode:|direct_prompt:|prompt:\\\"` before triggering a kickoff.\\n    85→\\n    86→---\\n    87→\\n    88→## 2026-04-16 — Issue numbers must be stamped in roadmap-data.ts before kickoff\\n    89→\\n    90→**Symptom:** Clicking \\\"Start\\\" creates a new duplicate GitHub Issue every time, even when the issue already exists.\\n    91→\\n    92→**Cause:** `createIssue()` is guarded by `item.issue ?? existing?.issue ?? null`. If `item.issue` is `undefined` in `roadmap-data.ts` AND Upstash Redis is not configured (so `existing` is always `{}`), the guard fails and a new issue is created unconditionally on every click.\\n    93→\\n    94→**Fix:** All issue numbers are now stamped in `\n\n...
